				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">

<table>
<table>

<tr>

</th>
<td>2
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1831 (Grand polonaise brillante), 1834 (Andante spianato)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Andantes&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Andantes</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Polonaises&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Polonaises</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li>The <i>Andante spianato</i> was first written for piano solo, but later orchestrated and added to the <i>Grande polonaise brillante</i> (which had been written in 1830-31) as an introduction.  The "new" <i>Grande polonaise brillante</i> was published in 1836.
</li></ul>
<table width="66%" align="center" style="font-size: 90%">

<tr>
<th colspan="2" align="center" style="background-color:rgb(155,204,0)"><b>Piano Music by <a href="/wiki/Category:Chopin,_Fr%C3%A9d%C3%A9ric" title="Category:Chopin, Frédéric">Frédéric Chopin</a></b>
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td valign="top" width="50%" style="background-color:rgb(155,222,120)">
<table class="collapsible collapsed" style="background-color:rgb(155,222,120)">
<tr>
<th><b>Polonaises</b>
</th></tr>
